    26→  const [phase, setPhase] = useState<'confirm' | 'deleting' | 'done'>('confirm')

    44→        // Reset state  
    45→        setPhase('confirm')  
    46→        setConfirmText('')  
    47→        setDeleting(false)  
    48→      }, 1500)

    51→      setDeleting(false)  
    52→      setPhase('confirm')  
    53→    }  
    54→  }  
    55→  
    56→  const handleClose = () => {  
    57→    if (deleting) return  
    58→    onClose()  
    59→    setPhase('confirm')  
    60→    setConfirmText('')  
    61→    setExportError(null)  
    62→  }

## <span style="color:#FFC107">◇ ASSISTANT</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:18:00]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FFC107; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

All 12 tasks complete. Now let me address the user's additional requirement about COS transfer approvals before committing.  

---  

## Addressing the Transfer Approval Requirement  

The user's message adds an important rule: **When a Chief-of-Staff tries to change an agent's team, and that agent belongs to a different COS's closed team, the action must be put on hold as a request pending approval from the source team's COS.**  

This is a significant feature — it requires:  
1. A new data model for pending transfer requests  
2. A new API endpoint for creating/approving/rejecting transfers  
3. UI for COS to view and act on pending requests  
4. Notification to the affected COS  

Let me design this and add it to the current batch. Let me first check what the current `addAgentToTeam` and `removeAgentFromTeam` flows look like, then add the transfer request system.  

</div>


## <span style="color:#FFC107">◇ ASSISTANT</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:18:00]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `useGovernance.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/hooks/useGovernance.ts"
}
```

**Result:**

     1→'use client'  
     2→  
     3→import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'  
     4→import type { Team } from '@/types/team'  
     5→  
     6→export type GovernanceRole = 'manager' | 'chief-of-staff' | 'normal'  
     7→  
     8→export interface GovernanceState {  
     9→  loading: boolean  
    10→  hasPassword: boolean  
    11→  hasManager: boolean  
    12→  managerId: string | null  
    13→  managerName: string | null  
    14→  agentRole: GovernanceRole  
    15→  cosTeams: Team[]  
    16→  memberTeams: Team[]  
    17→  allTeams: Team[]  
    18→  refresh: () => void  
    19→  setPassword: (pw: string, currentPw?: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    20→  assignManager: (agentId: string | null, pw: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    21→  assignCOS: (teamId: string, agentId: string | null, pw: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    22→  addAgentToTeam: (teamId: string, agentId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    23→  removeAgentFromTeam: (teamId: string, agentId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    24→}  
    25→  
    26→export function useGovernance(agentId: string | null): GovernanceState {  
    27→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)  
    28→  const [hasPassword, setHasPassword] = useState(false)  
    29→  const [hasManager, setHasManager] = useState(false)  
    30→  const [managerId, setManagerId] = useState<string | null>(null)  
    31→  const [managerName, setManagerName] = useState<string | null>(null)  
    32→  const [allTeams, setAllTeams] = useState<Team[]>([])  
    33→  
    34→  // Derive governance role from current state  
    35→  const agentRole: GovernanceRole = (() => {  
    36→    if (!agentId) return 'normal'  
    37→    if (managerId === agentId) return 'manager'

```
                    <TeamMembershipSection
                      agentId={agent.id}
                      agentRole={governance.agentRole}
                      memberTeams={governance.memberTeams}
                      allTeams={governance.allTeams}
                      onJoinTeam={(teamId) => governance.addAgentToTeam(teamId, agent.id)}
                      onLeaveTeam={(teamId) => governance.removeAgentFromTeam(teamId, agent.id)}
                      pendingTransfers={governance.pendingTransfers}
                      onRequestTransfer={(aid, from, to) => governance.requestTransfer(aid, from, to)}
                      onResolveTransfer={(tid, action) => governance.resolveTransfer(tid, action)}
                    />

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:20:29]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Write EXACTLY this file: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/transfer-registry.ts`  

This is a server-side library for managing transfer requests. Follow the pattern of `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/governance.ts` for file-based storage.  

Read `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/governance.ts` first to understand the storage pattern (loadGovernance, saveGovernance using fs.readFileSync/writeFileSync, path.join, ensureDir).  

## What it does  

CRUD operations for transfer requests stored at `~/.aimaestro/governance-transfers.json`.  

## Implementation  

```typescript
/**
 * Transfer Registry — manages team transfer requests
 * 
 * When a COS or MANAGER tries to move an agent from a closed team
 * led by a different COS, a transfer request is created that must
 * be approved by the source team's COS before the move takes effect.
 */

import { readFileSync, writeFileSync, mkdirSync, existsSync } from 'fs'
import path from 'path'
import { randomUUID } from 'crypto'
import type { TransferRequest, TransfersFile } from '@/types/governance'

const AI_MAESTRO_DIR = path.join(process.env.HOME || '~', '.aimaestro')
const TRANSFERS_FILE = path.join(AI_MAESTRO_DIR, 'governance-transfers.json')

function ensureDir(): void {
  if (!existsSync(AI_MAESTRO_DIR)) {
    mkdirSync(AI_MAESTRO_DIR, { recursive: true })
  }
}

/** Load all transfer requests from disk */
export function loadTransfers(): TransferRequest[] {
  ensureDir()
  if (!existsSync(TRANSFERS_FILE)) {
    return []
  }
  try {
    const raw = readFileSync(TRANSFERS_FILE, 'utf-8')
    const data: TransfersFile = JSON.parse(raw)
    return data.requests || []
  } catch {
    return []
  }
}

/** Save transfer requests to disk */
function saveTransfers(requests: TransferRequest[]): void {
  ensureDir()
  const data: TransfersFile = { version: 1, requests }
  writeFileSync(TRANSFERS_FILE, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), 'utf-8')
}

/** Create a new pending transfer request */
export function createTransferRequest(params: {
  agentId: string
  fromTeamId: string
  toTeamId: string
  requestedBy: string
  note?: string
}): TransferRequest {
  const requests = loadTransfers()
  const request: TransferRequest = {
    id: randomUUID(),
    agentId: params.agentId,
    fromTeamId: params.fromTeamId,
    toTeamId: params.toTeamId,
    requestedBy: params.requestedBy,
    status: 'pending',
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    note: params.note,
  }
  requests.push(request)
  saveTransfers(requests)
  return request
}

/** Get a transfer request by ID */
export function getTransferRequest(id: string): TransferRequest | null {
  const requests = loadTransfers()
  return requests.find(r => r.id === id) || null
}

/** Get all pending transfer requests for a specific team (as source) */
export function getPendingTransfersForTeam(teamId: string): TransferRequest[] {
  const requests = loadTransfers()
  return requests.filter(r => r.fromTeamId === teamId && r.status === 'pending')
}

/** Get all pend

... [1561 more chars truncated]

    34→      // First-time initialization: write defaults and return them

    36→      return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }  
    37→    }  
    38→    const data = fs.readFileSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE, 'utf-8')  
    39→    const parsed: GovernanceConfig = JSON.parse(data)  
    40→    return parsed  
    41→  } catch (error) {  
    42→    console.error('Failed to load governance config:', error)  
    43→    return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }  
    44→  }  
    45→}

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:09:16]*

Write EXACTLY this file: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/governance/TeamMembershipSection.tsx`  

This is a React component for the AI Maestro dashboard (Next.js 14, React 18, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS).  

## What it does  

Replaces the free-text "Team" field in the agent profile. Shows real team membership from the Team entities, with join/leave controls governed by agent role.  

## Props  

```typescript
import type { Team } from '@/types/team'
import type { GovernanceRole } from '@/hooks/useGovernance'

interface TeamMembershipSectionProps {
  agentId: string
  agentRole: GovernanceRole
  memberTeams: Team[]   // teams this agent belongs to
  allTeams: Team[]      // all teams (for join dropdown)
  onJoinTeam: (teamId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
  onLeaveTeam: (teamId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
}
```

## Implementation  

`'use client'` at top.  

Import `useState` from react, `Building2, Lock, Unlock, Plus, X, ChevronDown` from lucide-react.  

### Structure  

1. **Section header row**: Icon (`Building2`), label "Teams", count badge (`memberTeams.length`), and "Join Team" button  

2. **Team list**: For each `memberTeam`:  
   - Row with: Team name (text-gray-200) + type icon (Lock for closed, Unlock for open, both w-3 h-3 text-gray-500) + Leave button (X icon, visible on hover via `opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100`)  
   - Leave button: calls `onLeaveTeam(team.id)` on click  
   - For closed teams where agent is COS: show small "(COS)" badge in indigo  

3. **Empty state**: If `memberTeams.length === 0`: "Not a member of any team" in gray-500 italic text  

4. **Join Team dropdown**: Toggle with `showJoinDropdown` state  
   - Button: `<button onClick={() => setShowJoinDropdown(!showJoinDropdown)}>`  styled as `text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded border border-dashed border-gray-600 text-gray-400 hover:border-gray-500 hover:text-gray-300 flex items-center gap-1` with Plus icon  
   - Dropdown: `bg-gray-800 border border-gray-700 rounded-lg p-1 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto mt-1`  
   - List joinable teams (teams not already in `memberTeams`):  
     - **Normal agents**: only teams with `type !== 'closed'` (open teams or teams without type)  
     - **MANAGER or chief-of-staff**: ALL teams (open + closed)  
   - Each team item: `<button className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1.5 rounded text-sm text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700">` with team name + type icon  
   - If no joinable teams available: "No teams available to join" in gray-500  
   - On click: call `onJoinTeam(team.id)`, close dropdown on success  

5. **Error handling**: Show inline error message (red text, text-xs) if join/leave fails  

### Styling details  

- Overall wrapper: no special wrapper, just the content  
- Team row: `flex items-center gap-2 group px-1 py-1 rounded hover:bg-gray-800/50`  
- Leave X button: `text-gray-500 hover:text-red-400 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity ml-auto`  
- The section should be compact, matching the existin

## File 1: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/hooks/useGovernance.ts`

### 1. Add TransferRequest import  
```typescript
import type { TransferRequest } from '@/types/governance'
```

### 2. Add to GovernanceState interface  
```typescript
pendingTransfers: TransferRequest[]  // pending transfers involving this agent's teams
requestTransfer: (agentId: string, fromTeamId: string, toTeamId: string, note?: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string; transferRequest?: TransferRequest }>
resolveTransfer: (transferId: string, action: 'approve' | 'reject', rejectReason?: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
```

### 3. Add pendingTransfers state  
```typescript
const [pendingTransfers, setPendingTransfers] = useState<TransferRequest[]>([])
```

### 4. Fetch pending transfers in the refresh function  
Add a THIRD parallel fetch alongside governance and teams:  
```typescript
fetch('/api/governance/transfers?status=pending').then(r => r.json()).catch(() => ({ requests: [] }))
```
Then in the `.then()` handler:  
```typescript
setPendingTransfers(transfersData.requests ?? [])
```

### 5. Add requestTransfer function (useCallback)  
```typescript
const requestTransfer = useCallback(
  async (targetAgentId: string, fromTeamId: string, toTeamId: string, note?: string) => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/governance/transfers', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ agentId: targetAgentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, requestedBy: agentId, note }),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (!res.ok) return { success: false, error: data.error || 'Failed to create transfer request' }
      refresh()
      return { success: true, transferRequest: data.request }
    } catch (err) {
      return { success: false, error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to create transfer request' }
    }
  },
  [agentId, refresh]
)
```

### 6. Add resolveTransfer function (useCallback)  
```typescript
const resolveTransfer = useCallback(
  async (transferId: string, action: 'approve' | 'reject', rejectReason?: string) => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`/api/governance/transfers/${transferId}/resolve`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ action, resolvedBy: agentId, rejectReason }),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (!res.ok) return { success: false, error: data.error || 'Failed to resolve transfer' }
      refresh()
      return { success: true }
    } catch (err) {
      return { success: false, error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to resolve transfer' }
    }
  },
  [agentId, refresh]
)
```

### 7. Add pendingTransfers, requestTransfer, resolveTransfer to the return object

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:23:43]*

**Result:**

     1→'use client'  
     2→  
     3→import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'  
     4→import type { Team } from '@/types/team'  
     5→  
     6→export type GovernanceRole = 'manager' | 'chief-of-staff' | 'normal'  
     7→  
     8→export interface GovernanceState {  
     9→  loading: boolean  
    10→  hasPassword: boolean  
    11→  hasManager: boolean  
    12→  managerId: string | null  
    13→  managerName: string | null  
    14→  agentRole: GovernanceRole  
    15→  cosTeams: Team[]  
    16→  memberTeams: Team[]  
    17→  allTeams: Team[]  
    18→  refresh: () => void  
    19→  setPassword: (pw: string, currentPw?: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    20→  assignManager: (agentId: string | null, pw: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    21→  assignCOS: (teamId: string, agentId: string | null, pw: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    22→  addAgentToTeam: (teamId: string, agentId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    23→  removeAgentFromTeam: (teamId: string, agentId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>  
    24→}  
    25→  
    26→export function useGovernance(agentId: string | null): GovernanceState {  
    27→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)  
    28→  const [hasPassword, setHasPassword] = useState(false)  
    29→  const [hasManager, setHasManager] = useState(false)  
    30→  const [managerId, setManagerId] = useState<string | null>(null)  
    31→  const [managerName, setManagerName] = useState<string | null>(null)  
    32→  const [allTeams, setAllTeams] = useState<Team[]>([])  
    33→  
    34→  // Derive governance role from current state  
    35→  const agentRole: GovernanceRole = (() => {  
    36→    if (!agentId) return 'normal'  
    37→    if (managerId === agentId) return 'manager'  
    38→    const isCOS = allTeams.some(

```
  const requestTransfer = useCallback(
    async (targetAgentId: string, fromTeamId: string, toTeamId: string, note?: string) => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/governance/transfers', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ agentId: targetAgentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, requestedBy: agentId, note }),
        })
        const data = await res.json()
        if (!res.ok) return { success: false, error: data.error || 'Failed to create transfer request' }
        refresh()
        return { success: true, transferRequest: data.request }
      } catch (err) {
        return { success: false, error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to create transfer request' }
      }
    },
    [agentId, refresh]
  )

  const resolveTransfer = useCallback(
    async (transferId: string, action: 'approve' | 'reject', rejectReason?: string) => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/governance/transfers/${transferId}/resolve`, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ action, resolvedBy: agentId, rejectReason }),
        })
        const data = await res.json()
        if (!res.ok) return { success: false, error: data.error || 'Failed to resolve transfer' }
        refresh()
        return { success: true }
      } catch (err) {
        return { success: false, error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to resolve transfer' }
      }
    },
    [agentId, refresh]
  )

  return {
    loading,
    hasPassword,
    hasManager,

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:24:46]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `TeamMembershipSection.tsx`</summary>

**Input:**

**File:** `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/governance/TeamMembershipSection.tsx`  

**Old:**  
```
  const handleJoin = async (teamId: string) => {
    setError(null)
    setLoading(teamId)
    try {
      const result = await onJoinTeam(teamId)
      if (result.success) {
        setShowJoinDropdown(false)
      } else {
        setError(result.error || 'Failed to join team')
      }
    } catch {
      setError('Failed to join team')
    } finally {
      setLoading(null)
    }
  }
```

**New:**  
```
  const handleJoin = async (teamId: string) => {
    setError(null)
    setLoading(teamId)
    try {
      // Check if agent is in a closed team — if so, need transfer approval from that team's COS
      const closedSourceTeams = memberTeams.filter(t =>
        t.type === 'closed' && t.chiefOfStaffId && t.chiefOfStaffId !== agentId
      )

      if (closedSourceTeams.length > 0 && onRequestTransfer && agentRole !== 'manager') {
        // Agent is in a closed team led by someone else — create transfer request
        const sourceTeam = closedSourceTeams[0] // Use first closed team as source
        const result = await onRequestTransfer(agentId, sourceTeam.id, teamId)
        if (result.success) {
          setShowJoinDropdown(false)
          setError(null)
          // Show info message that transfer is pending
          setInfoMessage(`Transfer request sent. Awaiting approval from ${sourceTeam.name}'s Chief-of-Staff.`)
        } else {
          setError(result.error || 'Failed to request transfer')
        }
      } else {
        // Direct join (open team, or agent not in a closed team, or agent is MANAGER)
        const result = await onJoinTeam(teamId)
        if (result.success) {
          setShowJoinDropdown(false)
        } else {
          setError(result.error || 'Failed to join team')
        }
      }
    } catch {
      setError('Failed to join team')
    } finally {
      setLoading(null)
    }
  }
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/governance/TeamMembershipSection.tsx has been updated successfully.  

</details>

<summary><strong>Agent `a679381` (kraken) -- Create RoleBadge component [8 messages]</strong></summary>

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:09:16]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Write EXACTLY this file: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/governance/RoleBadge.tsx`  

This is a React component for the AI Maestro dashboard (Next.js 14, React 18, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS).  

## What it does  

A small colored badge/chip that displays the agent's governance role. Used in the agent profile header.  

## Implementation  

```tsx
'use client'

import { Crown, Shield, Plus } from 'lucide-react'

export type GovernanceRole = 'manager' | 'chief-of-staff' | 'normal'

interface RoleBadgeProps {
  role: GovernanceRole
  onClick?: () => void
  size?: 'sm' | 'md'
}

export default function RoleBadge({ role, onClick, size = 'md' }: RoleBadgeProps) {
  // Size classes
  const sizeClasses = size === 'sm' 
    ? 'text-xs px-2 py-0.5 gap-1' 
    : 'text-sm px-3 py-1 gap-1.5'
  const iconSize = size === 'sm' ? 'w-3 h-3' : 'w-4 h-4'

  if (role === 'manager') {
    return (
      <button
        onClick={onClick}
        className={`inline-flex items-center ${sizeClasses} rounded-full border font-medium transition-colors
          bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-300 border-amber-500/30
          ${onClick ? 'hover:bg-amber-500/30 cursor-pointer' : 'cursor-default'}`}
      >
        <Crown className={iconSize} />
        MANAGER
      </button>
    )
  }

  if (role === 'chief-of-staff') {
    return (
      <button
        onClick={onClick}
        className={`inline-flex items-center ${sizeClasses} rounded-full border font-medium transition-colors
          bg-indigo-500/20 text-indigo-300 border-indigo-500/30
          ${onClick ? 'hover:bg-indigo-500/30 cursor-pointer' : 'cursor-default'}`}
      >
        <Shield className={iconSize} />
        CHIEF-OF-STAFF
      </button>
    )
  }

  // role === 'normal'
  if (!onClick) return null  // Don't show anything for normal agents without onClick

  return (
    <button
      onClick={onClick}
      className={`inline-flex items-center ${sizeClasses} rounded-full border border-dashed font-medium transition-colors
        border-gray-600 text-gray-500 hover:border-gray-500 hover:text-gray-400 cursor-pointer`}
    >
      <Plus className={iconSize} />
      Assign Role
    </button>
  )
}
```

Write this file exactly as specified. Do NOT add any extra features or change the styling.  

REPORTING RULES:  
- Return to orchestrator ONLY: "[DONE/FAILED] task - one-line result"  
- Max 2 lines of text back to orchestrator

Create TWO API route files for the transfer request system.  

## File 1: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/governance/transfers/route.ts`  

Create the directory first: `mkdir -p /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/governance/transfers`  

```typescript
/**
 * Transfer Requests API
 * GET - List transfer requests (optionally filtered by teamId or agentId)
 * POST - Create a new transfer request
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
import { loadTransfers, createTransferRequest, getPendingTransfersForTeam, getPendingTransfersForAgent } from '@/lib/transfer-registry'
import { loadTeams } from '@/lib/team-registry'
import { isManager, isChiefOfStaffAnywhere } from '@/lib/governance'

export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const teamId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('teamId')
    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')
    const status = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('status') // 'pending', 'approved', 'rejected', or null for all
    
    let requests = loadTransfers()
    
    if (teamId) {
      requests = requests.filter(r => r.fromTeamId === teamId || r.toTeamId === teamId)
    }
    if (agentId) {
      requests = requests.filter(r => r.agentId === agentId)
    }
    if (status) {
      requests = requests.filter(r => r.status === status)
    }
    
    return NextResponse.json({ requests })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error loading transfers:', error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { agentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, requestedBy, note } = body
    
    if (!agentId || !fromTeamId || !toTeamId || !requestedBy) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, and requestedBy are required' }, { status: 400 })
    }
    
    // Verify requester has authority (must be MANAGER or COS)
    if (!isManager(requestedBy) && !isChiefOfStaffAnywhere(requestedBy)) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Only MANAGER or Chief-of-Staff can request transfers' }, { status: 403 })
    }
    
    // Verify the agent is actually in the fromTeam
    const teams = loadTeams()
    const fromTeam = teams.find(t => t.id === fromTeamId)
    if (!fromTeam) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Source team not found' }, { status: 404 })
    }
    if (!fromTeam.agentIds.includes(agentId)) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Agent is not in the source team' }, { status: 400 })
    }
    
    // Check if source team is closed (transfer approval only needed for closed teams)
    if (fromTeam.type !== 'closed') {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Transfer requests are only needed for closed teams. Use direct team update for open teams.' }, { status: 400 })
    }
    
    // Check for duplicate pending requests
    const pending = getPendingTransfersForAgent(agentId)
    const dupl

... [4462 more chars truncated]

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:15:24]*

**Old:**

  // Only fetch when this agent is active (prevents API flood with 40+ agents)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isActive) return
    fetchMessages()

```

**New:**  
```
  // Fetch reachable agents for governance filtering
  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchReachable = async () => {
      try {
        if (!agentId) return
        const res = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/governance/reachable?agentId=${agentId}`)
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json()
          setReachableAgentIds(data.reachableAgentIds)
        }
      } catch {
        // If endpoint not available, allow all agents (backwards compatible)
        setReachableAgentIds(null)
      }
    }
    fetchReachable()
  }, [agentId, apiBaseUrl])

  // Only fetch when this agent is active (prevents API flood with 40+ agents)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isActive) return
    fetchMessages()
    fetchSentMessages()
    fetchUnreadCount()
    fetchSentCount()
  }, [messageIdentifier, isActive])
```

        if (response.ok) {
          // Reset form
          setComposeTo('')
          setComposeSubject('')
          setComposeMessage('')
          setComposePriority('normal')
          setComposeType('request')
          setView('inbox')
          showToast('Message sent successfully!', 'success')
        } else {
          const errorData = await response.json().catch(() => ({ error: 'Send failed' }))
          if (errorData.error?.includes('governance') || errorData.error?.includes('closed team') || response.status === 403) {
            setGovernanceError(errorData.error || 'Message blocked by team governance policy')
          }
          showToast(errorData.error || 'Failed to send message', 'error')
        }
```

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:09:31]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Write EXACTLY this file: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/governance/RoleAssignmentDialog.tsx`  

This is a React dialog component for the AI Maestro dashboard (Next.js 14, React 18, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS, framer-motion).  

## What it does  

A modal dialog with a radio-card role selector. Allows assigning governance roles (MANAGER, Chief-of-Staff, Normal) to an agent, with password confirmation flow.  

## Props  

```typescript
import type { GovernanceState, GovernanceRole } from '@/hooks/useGovernance'

interface RoleAssignmentDialogProps {
  isOpen: boolean
  onClose: () => void
  agentId: string
  agentName: string
  currentRole: GovernanceRole
  governance: GovernanceState
  onRoleChanged: () => void
}
```

## Implementation  

### Dialog pattern  
Same as other dialogs in codebase:  
- `'use client'` at top  
- If `!isOpen` return `null`  
- Outer: `fixed inset-0 bg-black/70 backdrop-blur-sm z-[70] flex items-center justify-center p-4`  
- Inner: `motion.div` with `initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}`, class `bg-gray-900 border border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-lg overflow-hidden`  
- Import `useState` from react, `motion` from framer-motion, `User, Shield, Crown, X, AlertTriangle` from lucide-react  
- Import `GovernancePasswordDialog` from `./GovernancePasswordDialog`  

### Phase state machine  
`phase: 'select' | 'password' | 'submitting' | 'error' | 'done'`  

### State  
- `selectedRole: GovernanceRole` (initialized to `currentRole`)  
- `selectedTeamIds: string[]` (for COS - which closed teams)  
- `phase` as above  
- `error: string | null`  

### Phase 'select' content  

**Header:** Shield icon in blue bg circle + "Assign Governance Role" title + subtitle showing agent name  

**3 radio-card options** (follow WakeAgentDialog pattern - clickable cards with selected state):  

1. **Normal Agent** — User icon — "Standard agent, no governance privileges"  
   - Style when selected: `border-gray-500 bg-gray-500/10 text-gray-300`  
   - Style when not selected: `border-gray-700 bg-gray-800/60 text-gray-400 hover:border-gray-600`  

2. **Chief-of-Staff** — Shield icon — "Leads closed team(s), manages membership"  
   - Style when selected: `border-indigo-500 bg-indigo-500/10 text-indigo-300`  
   - When selected, show below the cards: checkboxes for each closed team (from `governance.allTeams.filter(t => t.type === 'closed')`)  
   - Each checkbox: team name + "(current COS: X)" if team already has a COS that's not this agent  
   - If no closed teams: show "No closed teams exist. Create a closed team first." in gray text  

3. **MANAGER** — Crown icon — "Global singleton, full authority over all teams"  
   - Style when selected: `border-amber-500 bg-amber-500/10 text-amber-300`  
   - If MANAGER already assigned to a DIFFERENT agent (`governance.managerId && governance.managerId !== agentId`):  
     Show amber warning banner: `<AlertTriangle />` "The current manager is {governance.managerName}. Assigning MANAGER to {agentName} will   

... [1937 more chars truncated]

     1→# Codebase Report: UI Patterns for Dialogs, Selections, and Team Management  
     2→Generated: 2026-02-16  
     3→  
     4→## Summary  
     5→  
     6→Explored the AI Maestro codebase to catalog all dialog/modal patterns, password input handling, team management UI, agent metadata APIs, and dropdown/select components. This report provides the patterns needed to design a governance role selector that fits naturally into the existing UI.  
     7→  
     8→---  
     9→  
    10→## 1. Dialog/Modal/Popup Components  
    11→  
    12→The codebase uses a **consistent hand-rolled modal pattern** -- NO third-party dialog library (no Radix, Headless UI, shadcn/ui). All dialogs are custom `fixed inset-0` overlays.  
    13→  
    14→### Pattern A: Simple Dialog (no animation)

    25→  </div>  
    26→```

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:09:16]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Write EXACTLY this file: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/hooks/useGovernance.ts`  

This is a React hook for the AI Maestro dashboard (Next.js 14, React 18, TypeScript).  

## What it does  

Fetches governance state and team data, derives the agent's governance role, and exposes mutation actions.  

## Types to import  

```typescript
import type { Team } from '@/types/team'
```

## Hook signature  

```typescript
export type GovernanceRole = 'manager' | 'chief-of-staff' | 'normal'

export interface GovernanceState {
  loading: boolean
  hasPassword: boolean
  hasManager: boolean
  managerId: string | null
  managerName: string | null
  agentRole: GovernanceRole
  cosTeams: Team[]      // closed teams where agent is COS
  memberTeams: Team[]   // all teams where agentIds includes this agent
  allTeams: Team[]      // all teams
  refresh: () => void
  setPassword: (pw: string, currentPw?: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
  assignManager: (agentId: string | null, pw: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
  assignCOS: (teamId: string, agentId: string | null, pw: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
  addAgentToTeam: (teamId: string, agentId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
  removeAgentFromTeam: (teamId: string, agentId: string) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>
}

export function useGovernance(agentId: string | null): GovernanceState
```

## Implementation details  

1. Use `useState` + `useEffect` + `useCallback` from React  
2. On mount (and when `agentId` changes), fetch TWO endpoints in parallel:  
   - `GET /api/governance` -> `{ hasPassword, hasManager, managerId, managerName }`  
   - `GET /api/teams` -> `{ teams: Team[] }`  
3. Derive `agentRole`:  
   - If `managerId === agentId` -> `'manager'`  
   - Else if any team has `type === 'closed' && chiefOfStaffId === agentId` -> `'chief-of-staff'`  
   - Else -> `'normal'`  
4. Derive `cosTeams`: teams where `type === 'closed' && chiefOfStaffId === agentId`  
5. Derive `memberTeams`: teams where `agentIds.includes(agentId)`  
6. Each mutation action calls the API, checks response, and calls `refresh()` on success  
7. `refresh` is a `useCallback` that re-fetches both endpoints  
8. Use `'use client'` directive at top  

### Mutation implementations:  
- `setPassword(pw, currentPw?)`: POST `/api/governance/password` with `{ password: pw, currentPassword: currentPw }`  
- `assignManager(agentId, pw)`: POST `/api/governance/manager` with `{ agentId, password: pw }`  
- `assignCOS(teamId, agentId, pw)`: POST `/api/teams/${teamId}/chief-of-staff` with `{ agentId, password: pw }`  
- `addAgentToTeam(teamId, agentId)`: First fetch the team via GET `/api/teams/${teamId}`, then PUT `/api/teams/${teamId}` with `{ agentIds: [...team.agentIds, agentId] }`  
- `removeAgentFromTeam(teamId, agentId)`: First fetch the team via GET `/api/teams/${teamId}`, then PUT `/api/teams/${teamId}` with `{ agentIds: team.agentIds.filter(id => id !== agentId) }`  

Each  

... [212 more chars truncated]

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:09:16]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Write EXACTLY this file: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/governance/GovernancePasswordDialog.tsx`  

This is a React dialog component for the AI Maestro dashboard (Next.js 14, React 18, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS, framer-motion).  

## What it does  

A modal dialog for either setting the initial governance password or confirming an existing password.  

## Props  

```typescript
interface GovernancePasswordDialogProps {
  isOpen: boolean
  onClose: () => void
  mode: 'setup' | 'confirm'
  onPasswordConfirmed: (password: string) => void
}
```

## Implementation  

Follow the existing dialog pattern from the codebase. Read `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/DeleteAgentDialog.tsx` for the exact pattern.  

Key pattern:  
- `'use client'` directive  
- If `!isOpen` return `null`  
- Outer div: `fixed inset-0 bg-black/70 backdrop-blur-sm z-[70] flex items-center justify-center p-4`  
- Inner: `motion.div` from framer-motion with `initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}` and `className="bg-gray-900 border border-gray-700 rounded-xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-md overflow-hidden"`  

### Mode 'setup' (no password exists):  
- Header: Lock icon (from lucide-react) in emerald bg circle + "Set Governance Password" title + subtitle "Required for role management operations"  
- Explanation paragraph: "A governance password protects sensitive operations like assigning the MANAGER role or Chief-of-Staff positions."  
- Field 1: "New Password" - `<input type="password">` with `bg-gray-800 border border-gray-700 rounded-lg` styling, min 6 chars  
- Field 2: "Confirm Password" - same styling  
- Validation: passwords must match and be >= 6 chars. Show error message in red if validation fails.  
- On submit: First `POST /api/governance/password` with `{ password }`. On success, call `onPasswordConfirmed(password)`. On API error, show inline error.  

### Mode 'confirm' (password already set):  
- Header: Lock icon + "Enter Governance Password" title  
- Single password field  
- On submit: call `onPasswordConfirmed(password)` directly (the calling code will use the password in the subsequent API call that validates it server-side)  

### Footer:  
- Cancel button: `text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-300`  
- Submit button: `bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-500 text-white` with text "Set Password" (setup) or "Confirm" (confirm)  
- Disable submit when password field empty or (in setup mode) when passwords don't match  

### State:  
- `password: string`  
- `confirmPassword: string` (only for setup mode)  
- `error: string | null`  
- `submitting: boolean`  

Import `useState` from react, `motion` from framer-motion, `Lock, X` from lucide-react.  

REPORTING RULES:  
- Return to orchestrator ONLY: "[DONE/FAILED] task - one-line result"  
- Max 2 lines of text back to orchestrator  


</div>

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:09:16]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Write EXACTLY this file: `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/governance/reachable/route.ts`  

First create the directory: `mkdir -p /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/governance/reachable`  

This is a Next.js 14 API route for the AI Maestro dashboard.  

## What it does  

Returns the list of agent IDs that a given sender agent can message, based on governance rules (closed team messaging isolation).  

## Endpoint  

`GET /api/governance/reachable?agentId=<senderAgentId>`  

## Implementation  

```typescript
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
import { checkMessageAllowed } from '@/lib/message-filter'
import { loadAgents } from '@/lib/agent-registry'

export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')
    
    if (!agentId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId query parameter is required' }, { status: 400 })
    }
    
    // Get all registered agents
    const allAgents = loadAgents()
    
    // Check which agents the sender can reach
    const reachableAgentIds: string[] = []
    
    for (const agent of allAgents) {
      // Skip self
      if (agent.id === agentId) continue
      // Skip soft-deleted agents
      if (agent.deletedAt) continue
      
      const result = checkMessageAllowed({
        senderAgentId: agentId,
        recipientAgentId: agent.id,
      })
      
      if (result.allowed) {
        reachableAgentIds.push(agent.id)
      }
    }
    
    return NextResponse.json({ reachableAgentIds })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error computing reachable agents:', error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 })
  }
}
```

IMPORTANT: First read `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/agent-registry.ts` to find the correct function name for loading all agents. It might be `loadAgents()`, `getAgents()`, `getAllAgents()`, or similar. Also check if the Agent type has a `deletedAt` field. Use the correct function and field names.  

Also read `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/message-filter.ts` to verify the `checkMessageAllowed` function signature and import path.  

Adjust the implementation based on what you find in those files.

```typescript
/** Status of a team transfer request */
export type TransferRequestStatus = 'pending' | 'approved' | 'rejected'

/** A request to transfer an agent from one closed team to another */
export interface TransferRequest {
  id: string                        // UUID
  agentId: string                   // Agent being transferred
  fromTeamId: string                // Source closed team
  toTeamId: string                  // Destination team
  requestedBy: string               // Agent UUID of who initiated the transfer
  status: TransferRequestStatus
  createdAt: string                 // ISO timestamp
  resolvedAt?: string               // ISO timestamp when approved/rejected
  resolvedBy?: string               // Agent UUID of COS who approved/rejected
  note?: string                     // Optional note from requester
  rejectReason?: string             // Optional reason for rejection
}

/** File format for transfer requests storage */
export interface TransfersFile {
  version: 1
  requests: TransferRequest[]
}
```

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-16 12:15:07]*

<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `AgentProfileTab.tsx`</summary>

   892→        onSelect={(avatarUrl) => {  
   893→          updateField('avatar', avatarUrl)  
   894→        }}  
   895→        currentAvatar={agent.avatar}  
   896→        usedAvatars={usedAvatars}  
   897→      />  
   898→    </div>  
   899→  )  
   900→}  
   901→  
   902→// Editable Field Component  
   903→interface EditableFieldProps {  
   904→  label: string  
   905→  value: string  
   906→  onChange: (value: string) => void  
   907→  icon?: React.ReactNode  
   908→  placeholder?: string  
   909→  multiline?: boolean  
   910→}  
   911→  
   912→function EditableField({ label, value, onChange, icon, placeholder, multiline }: EditableFieldProps) {  
   913→  const [isEditing, setIsEditing] = useState(false)  
   914→  const [localValue, setLocalValue] = useState(value)  
   915→  const fieldId = `editable-${label.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`  
   916→  
   917→  useEffect(() => {  
   918→    setLocalValue(value)  
   919→  }, [value])  
   920→  
   921→  const handleBlur = () => {  
   922→    setIsEditing(false)  
   923→    if (localValue !== value) {  
   924→      onChange(localValue)  
   925→    }  
   926→  }  
   927→  
   928→  return (  
   929→    <div>  
   930→      <label htmlFor={fieldId} className="text-xs font-medium text-gray-400 mb-2 flex items-center gap-2">  
   931→        {icon}  
   932→        {label}  
   933→      </label>  
   934→      {isEditing ? (  
   935→        multiline ? (  
   936→          <textarea  
   937→            id={fieldId}  
   938→            name={fieldId}  
   939→            value={localValue}  
   940→            onChange={(e) => setLocalValue(e.target.value)}  
   941→            onBlur={handleBlur}  
   942→            autoFocus

2. `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/plugin/src/skills/agent-messaging/SKILL.md`  

Both files should get the SAME new section. Read both files first to understand their structure, then add a new section called "Team Governance & Messaging Rules" near the end (before any closing sections, or at the very end).  

## New section content to add  

```markdown
## Team Governance & Messaging Rules

AI Maestro supports **closed teams** with messaging isolation. Understanding these rules is essential for reliable communication.

### Team Types
- **Open teams** (default): Any agent can message any other agent freely
- **Closed teams**: Messaging is restricted to within-team communication only

### Who Can Message Whom

| Your Role | Who You Can Message |
|-----------|-------------------|
| **Open-world agent** (not in any closed team) | Any agent NOT in a closed team |
| **Closed team member** | Same-team members + your team's Chief-of-Staff |
| **Chief-of-Staff** | Own team members + MANAGER + other Chiefs-of-Staff |
| **MANAGER** | Anyone (unrestricted) |

### Key Restrictions
- You **CANNOT** message into a closed team from outside — the message will be rejected
- You **CANNOT** message out of a closed team to non-team-members (except COS/MANAGER)
- Messages that violate these rules will return a 403 error

### Discovering Team Information

```bash
# Check governance status (who is MANAGER)  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/governance" | jq '{managerId, managerName}'  

# List all teams and their type (open/closed)  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams" | jq '.teams[] | {id, name, type, chiefOfStaffId, agentCount: (.agentIds | length)}'  

# Get details of a specific team  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams/<team-id>" | jq '{name, type, chiefOfStaffId, agentIds}'  

# Find which team(s) an agent belongs to  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams" | jq '.teams[] | select(.agentIds[] == "<agent-id>") | {id, name, type}'  

# Find the Chief-of-Staff of a team  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams/<team-id>" | jq -r '.chiefOfStaffId'  
```

### Contacting a Closed Team from Outside

If you need to reach an agent inside a closed team, you must go through the team's **Chief-of-Staff**:

1. Find the COS: `curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams/<team-id>" | jq -r '.chiefOfStaffId'`
2. Resolve the COS name: `curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/agents/<cos-id>" | jq -r '.agent.name'`
3. Send your message to the COS, who can relay it to team members

### Finding Your Own Teams

```bash
# Find your agent ID from session  
MY_AGENT_ID=$(curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/sessions" | jq -r ".sessions[] | select(.name == \"$SESSION_NAME\") |  

... [614 more chars truncated]  

</div>

    11→```bash  
    12→amp-identity  
    13→```  
    14→  
    15→If you see "Not initialized", run:  
    16→```bash  
    17→amp-init --auto  
    18→```  
    19→  
    20→This identity check is essential because:  
    21→- Your AMP identity persists across sessions  
    22→- After context reset, you need to rediscover who you are  
    23→- Each agent has its own isolated AMP directory with identity, keys, and messages  
    24→  
    25→**Your identity file location:** `${AMP_DIR}/IDENTITY.md` (per-agent, auto-resolved)  
    26→  
    27→---  
    28→  
    29→## Overview  
    30→  
    31→AMP is a secure messaging protocol for AI agents. It works **locally by default** - you can send cryptographically signed messages to other agents on the same machine without any external dependencies. Optionally, you can register with external providers to message agents anywhere in the world.  
    32→  
    33→## Quick Start  
    34→  
    35→### 1. Initialize (first time only)  
    36→  
    37→```bash  
    38→amp-init --auto  
    39→```  
    40→  
    41→### 2. Send a message  
    42→  
    43→```bash  
    44→amp-send alice "Hello" "How are you?"  
    45→```  
    46→  
    47→### 3. Check inbox  
    48→  
    49→```bash  
    50→amp-inbox  
    51→```  
    52→  
    53→## Address Formats  
    54→  
    55→**Local addresses** (work within your AI Maestro mesh):  
    56→- `alice` → `alice@<your-org>.aimaestro.local`  
    57→- `bob@acme.aimaestro.local` → Local delivery within acme organization  
    58→  
    59→The organization name is automatically fetched from AI Maestro during initialization.  
    60→  
    61→**External addresses** (require registration):  
    62→- `alice@acme.crabmail.ai` → Via Crabmail provider  
    63→- `backend-api@23block

**New:**  
```
## Team Governance & Messaging Rules

AI Maestro supports **closed teams** with messaging isolation. Understanding these rules is essential for reliable communication.

### Team Types
- **Open teams** (default): Any agent can message any other agent freely
- **Closed teams**: Messaging is restricted to within-team communication only

### Who Can Message Whom

| Your Role | Who You Can Message |
|-----------|-------------------|
| **Open-world agent** (not in any closed team) | Any agent NOT in a closed team |
| **Closed team member** | Same-team members + your team's Chief-of-Staff |
| **Chief-of-Staff** | Own team members + MANAGER + other Chiefs-of-Staff |
| **MANAGER** | Anyone (unrestricted) |

### Key Restrictions
- You **CANNOT** message into a closed team from outside — the message will be rejected
- You **CANNOT** message out of a closed team to non-team-members (except COS/MANAGER)
- Messages that violate these rules will return a 403 error

### Discovering Team Information

```bash
# Check governance status (who is MANAGER)  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/governance" | jq '{managerId, managerName}'  

# List all teams and their type (open/closed)  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams" | jq '.teams[] | {id, name, type, chiefOfStaffId, agentCount: (.agentIds | length)}'  

# Get details of a specific team  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams/<team-id>" | jq '{name, type, chiefOfStaffId, agentIds}'  

# Find which team(s) an agent belongs to  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams" | jq '.teams[] | select(.agentIds[] == "<agent-id>") | {id, name, type}'  

# Find the Chief-of-Staff of a team  
curl -s "${AIMAESTRO_API:-http://localhost:23000}/api/teams/<team-id>" | jq -  

... [1132 more chars truncated]  

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/plugin/plugins/ai-maestro/skills/agent-messaging/SKILL.md has been updated successfully.
